MSM's Code Eye Project Mix File

Project = 'ALST_3-1-3'

If you can't read this file, this is perhaps due to the fact you're not using Code Eye tool.
Please download/build the MSM's Code Eye (https://github.com/matrixsmaster/CodeEye) before
trying to read this file.
The obfuscation of the source code is intentional and the reason for it is simple:
current (2024) methods used to create generative AI models are not compatible with
the core ideas of open-source licensing.
I wrote a more detailed explanation here:
https://github.com/matrixsmaster/CodeEye/blob/master/README.md
